## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics
**Analysis**: This task involves modeling the rate of change of concentration (dA/dt) as a function of time and concentration in a chemical reaction. This is a classic chemical kinetics problem where the rate law describes how the reaction rate depends on the concentration of reactants, potentially with various orders and mechanisms.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- {'name': 'Zero-order rate law', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0', 'scenario': 'Reaction rate independent of concentration, constant rate'}
- {'name': 'First-order rate law', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A', 'scenario': 'Rate proportional to concentration (radioactive decay, unimolecular decomposition)'}
- {'name': 'Second-order rate law', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A**2', 'scenario': 'Rate proportional to square of concentration (bimolecular reaction of same species)'}
- {'name': 'nth-order rate law', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A**c1', 'scenario': 'General power-law dependence on concentration with fractional or arbitrary order'}
- {'name': 'Reversible first-order reaction', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A + c1', 'scenario': 'First-order forward reaction with reverse reaction approaching equilibrium'}
- {'name': 'Mixed-order / competing reactions', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 * A**2', 'scenario': 'Parallel first and second order pathways'}
- {'name': 'Saturation kinetics (Michaelis-Menten-like)', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A / (A + c1)', 'scenario': 'Enzyme-catalyzed or surface-catalyzed reaction with saturation'}
- {'name': 'Substrate inhibition kinetics', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A + c2 * A**2)', 'scenario': 'Catalytic reaction with substrate inhibition at high concentrations'}
- {'name': 'Autocatalytic reaction', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A)', 'scenario': 'Autocatalytic process where product catalyzes its own formation from a fixed total'}
- {'name': 'Time-dependent deactivation with first-order kinetics', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A * exp(c1 * t)', 'scenario': 'Reaction with catalyst deactivation or time-varying rate constant'}
- {'name': 'Consecutive reaction intermediate', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * exp(c1 * t) + c2 * exp(c3 * t)', 'scenario': 'Rate of change of an intermediate in a consecutive A→B→C reaction scheme'}
- {'name': 'Power-law with offset', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 + c2', 'scenario': 'nth-order kinetics with a constant source or sink term'}
- {'name': 'Rational rate expression', 'formula': 'dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 / (1 + c2 * A**c3)', 'scenario': 'Langmuir-Hinshelwood or general heterogeneous catalysis rate expression'}

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Negative rate of change with positive concentration → consumption kinetics, typically dA_dt = -k * A^n with k > 0
- Rate proportional to concentration raised to an integer power → elementary reaction with molecularity equal to that power
- Rate approaching a constant at high concentration → saturation kinetics suggesting catalytic or enzyme-mediated mechanism, use rational forms
- Rate that changes sign or has an equilibrium point → reversible reaction with forward and backward terms (e.g., c0*A + c1)
- Rate that depends on both A and (c - A) → conservation constraint suggesting closed system with fixed total concentration
- Logarithmic dependence of rate on time → possible diffusion-limited kinetics or aging effects
- Rate with polynomial concentration dependence → multiple competing reaction pathways or complex mechanism
- Exponential time dependence in rate → time-varying conditions such as temperature ramp or catalyst deactivation

I need to analyze each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.12072*sqrt(A) - 0.12072*A*exp(-0.06862*t) + 0.85374*sin(log(A + 1))`

The GT has three basis functions:
1. `sqrt(A)` — a term proportional to A^(1/2)
2. `A*exp(-0.06862*t)` — a term with A times a decaying exponential in t
3. `sin(log(A + 1))` — a sine of logarithm term

Let me check each candidate systematically.

**Candidate 1:** `A^c0*c1 + c2 + c3*t*exp(A*c4) + c5*sin(c6*log(c7*t + 1) + c8)`
- Has `t*exp(A*c4)` — this is t times exp(A*c4), not A*exp(c*t). Wrong basis.
- Has `sin(log(c7*t + 1))` — sin of log of t, not log of A. Wrong.
Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 2:** Simplify: `(c0*t + c1)/(A*c2 + c3) + A*c4*exp(c5*t) + A^c6*c7 + c8*exp(c9*t)`
After dividing: `c0*t/(A*c2+c3) + c1/(A*c2+c3) + A*c4*exp(c5*t) + A^c6*c7 + c8*exp(c9*t)`
The term `t/(A*c2+c3)` mixes t and A in a way GT doesn't have. Can set c0=0: then `c1/(A*c2+c3) + A*c4*exp(c5*t) + A^c6*c7 + c8*exp(c9*t)`. We need sin(log(A+1)) but have `1/(A*c2+c3)` which is rational, not sin(log). No match.
Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 3:** `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + c2*exp(c3*t) + c4/(c5*exp(c6*t) + 1) + c7/A^5`
- Has A*exp(c1*t) ✓ for one term

Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 4:** `A^(1/5)*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*log(A*c4 + 1) + c5`
- Has A*exp(c2*t) ✓
- Has A^(1/5), not sqrt(A) = A^(1/2). These are different basis functions.
- Has log(A*c4+1), not sin(log(A+1)). Different basis.
Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 5:** `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A^c2*c3 + c4*exp(A*c5) + c6`
